A dictionary of terms in the [[Low Alöbi]] language.

# a
### -a

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-a|*-a]]_.
> ¹ Adjunct
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-a|-a]]_
### abta
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑbtɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑbdɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [abdə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*apta|*apta]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ap|*ap]]_ ("lay out, arrange") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Laid out flat; ² Arranged in a particular way
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#abda|abda]]_
### acas
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑˑtʃɑs]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑdʒɑs]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [adʒəs]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*acas|*acas]]_.
> ¹ Snake
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ajas|ajas]]_
### acok'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑˑtʃokʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑdʒɔkʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [adʒɔkʼ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*acuk'|*acuk']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*cuq'|*cuq']]_ ("stone").
> ¹ Stone
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ajok|ajok]]_
### acowmö
ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [adʒowmœ]

*num.* From _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#acö|acö]]_ ("one") + _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#omö|omö]]_ ("five").
> ¹ Six
### acö
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑˑtʃø]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑdʒœ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [adʒœ]

*num.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔacü|*ʔacü]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔac|*ʔac]]_ ("one").
> ¹ One
> **Derivatives:** _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#acowmö|acowmö]]_ ("six")
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#újö|újö]]_
### -ag

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ag|*-ag]]_.
> ¹ Numeral classifier used to count smaller land animals that are typically considered edible such as [[K'übi]], flightless birds and big toads
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-on|-on]]_
### agök
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑˑŋøk]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑŋœk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [aŋœk]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*agük|*agük]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ag|*ag]]_ ("open") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ük|*ük]]_ ("split").
> ¹ To split open
### agta
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑɴtɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑ̃ndɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ɔ̃ndə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*agta|*agta]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ag|*ag]]_ ("open") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Opened up, as of a flower
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#onda|onda]]_
### aib
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑˑib]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑjb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ajb]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ayip|*ayip]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ip|*ip]]_ ("thin, narrow").
> ¹ Narrow gap
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#eb|eb]]_
### aigem
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑˑiŋəm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑjŋə̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ajŋɛ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ayīgem|*ayīgem]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*īg|*īg]]_ ("enter") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Entrance; ² Door
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#egen|egen]]_
### ainklos
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑˑinklos]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑɪ̃ŋklɔs]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ajŋklɔs]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ayinqrus|*ayinqrus]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*inqrus|*inqrus]]_ ("the sun").
> ¹ Sunlight
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#enklos|enklos]]_
### akyaw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑˑkjɑw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑkjɑw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [akjaw]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*akyaw|*akyaw]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kyaw|*kyaw]]_ ("scream").
> ¹ To screech, caw; ² To scream, call out
### alig
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑˑliŋ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑlɪ̃ŋ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [alɪ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔalīg|*ʔalīg]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔal-|*ʔal-]]_ ("outside, outer") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*īg|*īg]]_ ("enter").
> ¹ To exit a building, cave or other enclosed space
### alt'ak'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑltʼɑqʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑɫtʼɑqʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [awtʼəqʼ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔalt'aq'|*ʔalt'aq']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔal-|*ʔal-]]_ ("outside, outer") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'aq'|*t'aq']]_ ("shell").
> ¹ Shell of an animal
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#otak|otak]]_
### ama
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑˑmɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑmɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [amə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔama|*ʔama]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔam|*ʔam]]_ ("more").
> ¹ Bigger than
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ama|ama]]_
### amam
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑˑmɑm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑmɑ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [amɔ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*amam|*amam]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*am|*am]]_ ("house") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("specifier").
> ¹ Hut
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#amon|amon]]_
### amel
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑˑməl]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑməɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [amaw]

> ¹ To compare to; ² To weigh
### amkis

> ¹ To be above
### amküc'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑmkytʃʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑ̃ŋkʏtʃʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ɔ̃ŋkʏtʃʼ]

> ¹ To be higher than
### amk'i
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑmkʼi]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑ̃ŋkʼɪ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ɔ̃ŋkʼɪ]

### amk'öy
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑmkʼøj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑ̃ŋkʼœj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ɔ̃ŋkʼej]

### amlih

### amök'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑˑmøkʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑmœkʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [amœkʼ]

### amöt

> ¹ To be exactly equal to; ² To be roughly equivalent to
### ana
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑˑnɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑnɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [anə]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*anaʔ|*anaʔ]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*naq|*naq]]_ ("eat").
> ¹ To eat
> **Derivatives:** _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#anaqa|anaqa]]_ ("mouth, opening")
### anaqa
ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑnɑʔɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [anəʔə]

*n.* From _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#ana|ana]]_ ("to eat"). Perhaps related to [[Low Alöbi]] _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#kiaq|kiaq]]_ ("to bite"), [[Xiri]] _[[Xiri dictionary#na’a|na’a]]_ ("mouth").
> ¹ Mouth, opening
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ana|ana]]_
### anök
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑˑnøk]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑnœk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [anœk]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*anük|*anük]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<an>|*<an>]]_ ("instrument") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ük|*ük]]_ ("split").
> ¹ Axe
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#anök|anök]]_
### anxub
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑnʃub]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑ̃nʃʊb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ɔ̃ːʃʊb]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*anxūp|*anxūp]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<an>|*<an>]]_ ("instrument") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xūp|*xūp]]_ ("adze").
> ¹ Adze, a tool used to hollow out a log into a canoe
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#onxub|onxub]]_
### aqaq
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑˑʔɑʔ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑʔɑʔ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [aʔəʔ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*aqaq|*aqaq]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*aq|*aq]]_ ("bite, chew") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("repetitively").
> ¹ To chew
### atüm
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑˑtym]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑdʏ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [adʊ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*atyǖm|*atyǖm]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tyǖm|*tyǖm]]_ ("pouch, pocket").
> ¹ Pouch, pocket
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#adun|adun]]_
### aül
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑˑyl]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑʏɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [aew]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔayǖr|*ʔayǖr]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔǖr|*ʔǖr]]_ ("night").
> ¹ Nighttime
> **Derivatives:** _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#aülinklos|aülinklos]]_ ("nighttime sun")
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#eli|eli]]_
### aülinklos
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑˑylinklos]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑʏlɪ̃ŋklɔs]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [aʏlɪ̃ŋklɔs]

*n.* From _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#aül|aül]]_ ("nighttime") + _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#inklos|inklos]]_ ("the sun").
> ¹ The nighttime sun, a name for [[Bigmoon]] in its full phase
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ölinklos|ölinklos]]_
### awa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑˑwɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑwɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [awə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*agwa|*agwa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ag|*ag]]_ ("open") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser").
> ¹ Open, as of a mouth or cave
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ova|ova]]_
### awi
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑˑwi]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑwɪ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [awɪ]

> ¹ Flower
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ovi|ovi]]_
### -ay

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ay|*-ay]]_.
> ¹ Numeral classifier used to count pieces of a segmental structure such as teeth, scales, words and units of time
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-e|-e]]_
### ayag
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑˑjɑɴ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑjɑ̃ɴ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ajɔ̃ː]

### ayamem
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑˑjɑməm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑjɑmə̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ajəmɛ̃ː]

### aylib
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑjlib]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑjlɪb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ajlɪb]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔaylip|*ʔaylip]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔlip|*ʔlip]]_ ("meteor, comet").
> ¹ Meteor shower
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#elib|elib]]_, [[Xiri]] _[[Xiri dictionary#airi|airi]]_ ("meteor")
### ayom
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑˑjom]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑjɔ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ajɔ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔayum|*ʔayum]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔal|*ʔal]]_ ("outside") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Outdoors; ² Forest
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#eyon|eyon]]_
### aywam
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑjwɑm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑjwɑ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ajwɔ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔaywam|*ʔaywam]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔwam|*ʔwam]]_ ("firmament").
> ¹ The celestial sphere, the surface on which the stars and celestial bodies lie
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#evon|evon]]_ ("the sky")
# b
### babay
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bɑˑbɑj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bɑbɑj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [babaj]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*papay|*papay]]_.
> ¹ Layer; ² Coating
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#babe|babe]]_
### bac'ük
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bɑˑtʃʼyk]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bɑtʃʼʏk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [batʃʼʏk]

> ¹ To break
### bamay
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bɑˑmɑj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bɑmɑj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [bamaj]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pamay|*pamay]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pa-|*pa-]]_ ("gather or obtain") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*may|*may]]_ ("know, remember").
> ¹ To research, gather knowledge; ² To develop an understanding
### bamit

### banat'

### cihwa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʃiˑxʷɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʃiɸɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʃiɸə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*cihwa|*cihwa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*cih|*cih]]_ ("divide") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser").
> ¹ Separated, far apart
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#jífa|jífa]]_
### cikü

### cimcim

### cisk'on

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*c'ūk'a|*c'ūk'a]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*c'ūk'|*c'ūk']]_ ("hit").
> ¹ Hard
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#cúka|cúka]]_
### c'uk'em
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʃʼuˑkʼəm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʃʼukʼə̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʃʼukʼɛ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*c'ūk'em|*c'ūk'em]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*c'ūk'|*c'ūk']]_ ("hit") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Drum
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#cúken|cúken]]_
### c'übem
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʃʼyˑbəm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʃʼybə̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʃʼybɛ̃ː]

> ¹ Peelings, of tubers or certain fruit

### eal
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [eˑɑl]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [eɑɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [eaw]

### ean

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ep|*-ep]]_ ("oblique"), Perhaps related to [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-iw|*-iw]]_ ("oblique").
> ¹ Oblique case
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-v|-v]]_ ("oblique")

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-en|*-en]]_.
> ¹ Numeral classifier used to count roundish lumps that fit in the hand such as round fruit and vegetables, pieces of meat and large eggs

### gayaw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɴɑˑjɑw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɴɑjɑw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ɴajaw]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gayaw|*gayaw]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gaw|*gaw]]_ ("north-easterly wind").
> ¹ Dry season
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#geyo|geyo]]_
### gaywacma
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɴɑjwɑtʃmɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɴɑjwɑdʒmɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ɴajwədʒmə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gaywacma|*gaywacma]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gwac|*gwac]]_ ("far away") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Infinite
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#gevajma|gevajma]]_
### gic'em
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ŋiˑtʃʼəm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ŋitʃʼə̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ŋitʃʼɛ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gic'em|*gic'em]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gic'|*gic']]_ ("immovable") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Immovable object
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#gícen|gícen]]_
### gilbu
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ŋilbu]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ŋɪɫbʊ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ŋewbʊ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gilpū|*gilpū]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gil|*gil]]_ ("moon") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pū|*pū]]_ ("elder sibling").
> ¹ The larger of the two moons of winter
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#göbu|göbu]]_
### gilki
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ŋilki]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ŋɪɫkɪ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ŋewkɪ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gilki|*gilki]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gil|*gil]]_ ("moon") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ki|*ki]]_ ("younger sibling").
> ¹ The smaller of the two moons of winter
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#göki|göki]]_
### gilmö
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ŋilmø]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ŋɪɫmœ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ŋewmœ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gilmü|*gilmü]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gil|*gil]]_ ("moon") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*mü|*mü]]_ ("cycle").
> ¹ A minor month, equal to 10 days
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#gömö|gömö]]_
### gosum
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ŋoˑsum]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ŋosʊ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ŋosʊ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gusūm|*gusūm]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*sūm|*sūm]]_ ("remove").
> ¹ To remove
### gük
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ŋyk]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ŋʏk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ŋʏk]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gǖk|*gǖk]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gaw|*gaw]]_ ("north-easterly wind") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ek|*-ek]]_ ("animate object nominaliser").
> ¹ North-easterly wind
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#gök|gök]]_
# h
### habom
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [χɑˑbom]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [χɑbɔ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [χabɔ̃ː]

> ¹ To ripen
### haim
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [χɑˑim]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [χɑɪ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [χaj]

> ¹ Bed; ² Bedroom, personal quarters
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#he|he]]_
### hamog
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [χɑˑmoŋ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [χɑmɔ̃ŋ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [χamɔ̃ː]

> ¹ To keep trying, working towards something
### hamök'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [χɑˑmøkʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [χɑmœkʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [χamœkʼ]

> ¹ To grow old
### hamök'et
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [χɑˑmøkʼət]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [χɑmœkʼət]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [χamœkʼət]

> ¹ Old person
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#hankat|hankat]]_
### hamöl
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [χɑˑmøl]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [χɑmœɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [χamew]

> ¹ To develop a skill; ² To learn something
### hamön
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [χɑˑmøn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [χɑmœ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [χamɔ̃ː]

### hilap'

### honu

### hüma

### hwaten

### hyac'ek
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [çɑˑtʃʼək]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɕɑtʃʼək]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ɕatʃʼək]

# i
### -i

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-i|*-i]]_.
> ¹ Relational linker
> **Derivatives:** _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#k'ak'ohümi|k'ak'ohümi]]_ ("wagon house")
### iba
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [iˑbɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ibɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ibə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ipa|*ipa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ip|*ip]]_ ("thin, narrow").
> ¹ Thin, narrow; ² Skinny, as of a person
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#íba|íba]]_
### ibib
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [iˑbib]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ibɪb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ibɪb]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ipip|*ipip]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ip|*ip]]_ ("thin, narrow") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("specifier").
> ¹ Fur of an animal
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#íbib|íbib]]_
### ibyal
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [iˑbjɑl]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ibjɑɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ibjaw]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ipyar|*ipyar]]_.
> ¹ To cross over; ² To travel through
### ica
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [iˑtʃɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [idʒɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [idʒə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔica|*ʔica]]_ ("wide"), from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔic|*ʔic]]_ ("wide, broad").
> ¹ Long
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#íja|íja]]_
### icab
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [iˑtʃɑb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [idʒɑb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [idʒəb]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔicap|*ʔicap]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔic|*ʔic]]_ ("wide, broad") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ap|*ap]]_ ("lay out, arrange").
> ¹ To lay out flat; ² To position far apart
### icaqa
ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [idʒɑʔɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [idʒəʔə]

*stat.* From _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#ici|ici]]_ ("pig").
> ¹ Fat, as of a person
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#íca|íca]]_
### ichamön
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [itʃχɑmøn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɪtʃχɑmœ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ɪtʃχəmɔ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔichamyün|*ʔichamyün]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔic'-|*ʔic'-]]_ ("upwards") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*hamyün|*hamyün]]_ ("to grow, develop").
> ¹ To grow, as of a plant
### ici
ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [idʒɪ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [idʒɪ]

*n.* From [[Xiri]] _[[Xiri dictionary#iji|iji]]_, from [[Proto-Xiric language|Proto-Xiric]] _[[Proto-Xiric dictionary#\*eici|*eici]]_.
> ¹ Pig
> **Derivatives:** _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#icaqa|icaqa]]_ ("fat")
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#íji|íji]]_
### icköc
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [itʃkøtʃ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɪtʃkœtʃ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ɪtʃkœtʃ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔicküc|*ʔicküc]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔic'-|*ʔic'-]]_ ("upwards") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*küc|*küc]]_ ("stand").
> ¹ To stand up
### ictaw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [itʃtɑw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɪtʃtɑw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ɪtʃtaw]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔictaw|*ʔictaw]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔic'-|*ʔic'-]]_ ("upwards") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*taw|*taw]]_ ("carry").
> ¹ To pick up; ² To carry
### icwa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [iˑtʃwɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [idʒwɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [idʒwə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*icwa|*icwa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ic|*ic]]_ ("hunger") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser").
> ¹ Hungry
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#íjva|íjva]]_
### ic'ik'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [iˑtʃʼikʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [itʃʼɪkʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [itʃʼɪkʼ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔic'yik'|*ʔic'yik']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔic'-|*ʔic'-]]_ ("upwards") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yik'|*yik']]_ ("pluck, uproot").
> ¹ To uproot vegetables
### iget
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [iˑŋət]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [iŋət]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [iŋət]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*īget|*īget]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*īg|*īg]]_ ("enter") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Door
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ígat|ígat]]_
### igi
ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [iŋɪ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [iŋɪ]

*n.* From [[Xiri]] _[[Xiri dictionary#igi|igi]]_, from [[Proto-Xiric language|Proto-Xiric]] _[[Proto-Xiric dictionary#\*iqi|*iqi]]_.
> ¹ Milk
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ígi|ígi]]_
### iha
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [iˑχɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [iχɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [iχə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yiha|*yiha]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yih|*yih]]_ ("feather").
> ¹ Feathered; ² Ornately decorated
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#íha|íha]]_
### ihbaü
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ixbɑy]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɪxbɑj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ɪxbaj]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yihpaǖ|*yihpaǖ]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yih|*yih]]_ ("feather") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*paǖ|*paǖ]]_ ("tree") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-i|*-i]]_ ("relational linker").
> ¹ Leaf, leaves
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ihpe|ihpe]]_
### ihih
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [iˑxix]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ixɪx]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ixɪx]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yihyih|*yihyih]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yih|*yih]]_ ("feather") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("specifier").
> ¹ Feathers; ² Wing
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#íhih|íhih]]_
### ikban
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ikbɑn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɪkbɑ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ɪkbɔ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ikpan|*ikpan]]_.
> ¹ [[Ikban]], a small [[Wug]], similar to antelopes
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ikpon|ikpon]]_
### ik'ik'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [iˑkʼikʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ikʼɪkʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ikʼɪkʼ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yik'yik'|*yik'yik']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yik'|*yik']]_ ("pluck, uproot") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("repetitively").
> ¹ To pluck feathers from a bird
### ilama
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [iˑlɑmɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ilɑmɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [iləmə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔilama|*ʔilama]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<il>|*<il>]]_ ("result or product") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔam|*ʔam]]_ ("more").
> ¹ Most, many
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#öma|öma]]_
### imim
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [iˑmim]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [imɪ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [imɪ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔimʔim|*ʔimʔim]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔim|*ʔim]]_ ("cloud") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("specifier").
> ¹ Cloud cover; ² Cloud
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ímin|ímin]]_
### -in

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-in|*-in]]_ ("ergative").
> ¹ Ergative case
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-in|-in]]_ ("ergative")
### ina
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [iˑnɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [inɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [inə]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*inna|*inna]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*in-|*in-]]_ ("characteristic agent") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*na|*na]]_ ("parent").
> ¹ Parent
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ína|ína]]_
### inbu
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [inbu]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɪ̃mbʊ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ɪ̃mbʊ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*inpū|*inpū]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*in-|*in-]]_ ("characteristic agent") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pū|*pū]]_ ("elder sibling").
> ¹ Elder sibling; ² The larger of the two moons of Winter
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#inbu|inbu]]_
### inki
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [inki]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɪ̃ŋkɪ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ɪ̃ŋkɪ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*inki|*inki]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*in-|*in-]]_ ("characteristic agent") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ki|*ki]]_ ("younger sibling").
> ¹ Younger sibling; ² The smaller of the two moons of Winter
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#inki|inki]]_
### inklos
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [inklos]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɪ̃ŋklɔs]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ɪ̃ŋklɔs]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*inqrus|*inqrus]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*in-|*in-]]_ ("characteristic agent") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qrus|*qrus]]_ ("day").
> ¹ The sun
> **Derivatives:** _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#aülinklos|aülinklos]]_ ("nighttime sun")
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#inklos|inklos]]_
### inö
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [iˑnø]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [inœ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [inœ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*innü|*innü]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*in-|*in-]]_ ("characteristic agent") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*nü|*nü]]_ ("see").
> ¹ Eye
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ínö|ínö]]_
### int'ib
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [intʼib]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɪ̃ntʼɪb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ɪ̃ntʼɪb]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*int'ip|*int'ip]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*in-|*in-]]_ ("characteristic agent") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'i|*t'i]]_ ("small") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ep|*-ep]]_ ("person object nominaliser").
> ¹ Child
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#intib|intib]]_
### inül
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [iˑnyl]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [inʏɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [inew]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*inʔǖr|*inʔǖr]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*in-|*in-]]_ ("characteristic agent") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔǖr|*ʔǖr]]_ ("night").
> ¹ Either or both of the two moons of Winter
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#íno|íno]]_
### inwit'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [iˑnwitʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [imɪtʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [imɪtʼ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*inwit'|*inwit']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*in-|*in-]]_ ("characteristic agent") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wit'|*wit']]_ ("different, other").
> ¹ Addressee
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ímit|ímit]]_
### inya
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [iˑɲɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [iɲɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [iɲə]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*innya|*innya]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*in-|*in-]]_ ("characteristic agent") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*nya|*nya]]_ ("sound").
> ¹ Ear
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#íña|íña]]_
### ititen
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [iˑtitən]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [idɪdə̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [idɪdɛ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ititen|*ititen]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*it|*it]]_ ("foot, hoof") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("specifier") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-en|*-en]]_ ("possessed").
> ¹ Centipede
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#íden|íden]]_
### -iw

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-iw|*-iw]]_.
> ¹ Numeral classifier used to count flying birds
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-ö|-ö]]_
### iwab
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [iˑwɑb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [iwɑb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [iwəb]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*iwap|*iwap]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*iw-|*iw-]]_ ("distributed") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ap|*ap]]_ ("lay out, arrange").
> ¹ To arrange in a particular way
### iwan
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [iˑwɑn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [iwɑ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [iwɔ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yīwan|*yīwan]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<īw>|*<īw>]]_ ("internal organ") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yan|*yan]]_ ("within, inside").
> ¹ Stomach
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ívon|ívon]]_
### iwbak
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [iwbɑq]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɪwbɑq]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ewbəq]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*iwpak|*iwpak]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*iw-|*iw-]]_ ("distributed") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pak|*pak]]_ ("animal").
> ¹ Herd of animals
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#öbak|öbak]]_
### iwbüc
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [iwbytʃ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɪwbʏtʃ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ewbʏtʃ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*iwpǖc|*iwpǖc]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*iw-|*iw-]]_ ("distributed") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pǖc|*pǖc]]_ ("decorate").
> ¹ To decorate ornately
### iwcih
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [iwtʃix]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɪwdʒɪx]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ewdʒɪx]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*iwcih|*iwcih]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*iw-|*iw-]]_ ("distributed") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*cih|*cih]]_ ("divide").
> ¹ To divide, split up
### iwkib
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [iwkib]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɪwkɪb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ewkɪb]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*iwkip|*iwkip]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*iw-|*iw-]]_ ("distributed") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kip|*kip]]_ ("squirt").
> ¹ To spray; ² To splatter
### iwp'löc
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [iwpʼløtʃ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɪwpʼlœtʃ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ewpʼlœtʃ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*iwp'lüc|*iwp'lüc]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*iw-|*iw-]]_ ("distributed") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*p'lüc|*p'lüc]]_ ("scatter").
> ¹ To scatter
### iwp'üh
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [iwpʼyxʷ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɪwpʼʏɸ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ewpʼʏɸ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*iwp'ǖh|*iwp'ǖh]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*iw-|*iw-]]_ ("distributed") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*p'ǖh|*p'ǖh]]_ ("swarm").
> ¹ Swarm of insects
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#öpöf|öpöf]]_
### iwtob

### kömtyag
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kømcɑɴ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kœ̃ɲɟɑ̃ɴ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kɔ̃ɲɟɔ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kümtyag|*kümtyag]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*küm|*küm]]_ ("face, front part") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tyag|*tyag]]_ ("bone").
> ¹ Lower jaw
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#konjon|konjon]]_
### kuhamön
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kuˑχɑmøn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kuχɑmœ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kuχəmɔ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kwūhamyün|*kwūhamyün]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kwū-|*kwū-]]_ ("radially outwards") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*hamyün|*hamyün]]_ ("to grow, develop").
> ¹ To expand in size
### kula
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kuˑlɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kulɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kulə]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kwūra|*kwūra]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kwū-|*kwū-]]_ ("radially outwards") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ra|*ra]]_ ("smell, taste").
> ¹ To smell
### kulis
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kuˑlis]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kuɫs]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kows]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kwūlis|*kwūlis]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kwū-|*kwū-]]_ ("radially outwards") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*lis|*lis]]_ ("light").
> ¹ To radiate light
### kuso
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kuˑso]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kusɔ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kusɔ]

*pron.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kūsu|*kūsu]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ke-|*ke-]]_ ("dual") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*usu|*usu]]_ ("second person").
> ¹ Second person dual
### küc'a
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kyˑtʃʼɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kytʃʼɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kytʃʼə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kǖc'a|*kǖc'a]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kǖc'|*kǖc']]_ ("high").
> ¹ High up, as of a cliff or cloud; ² Far down
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kíca|kíca]]_
### kük
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kyk]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kʏk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kʏk]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qwǖk|*qwǖk]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qwiw|*qwiw]]_ ("south-easterly monsoon wind") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ek|*-ek]]_ ("animate object nominaliser").
> ¹ South-easterly monsoon wind
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kök|kök]]_
### kükü
ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kykʏ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kykʏ]

*n.* From [[Xiri]] _[[Xiri dictionary#kwi|kwi]]_ ("yam"), from [[Proto-Xiric language|Proto-Xiric]] _[[Proto-Xiric dictionary#\*kue|*kue]]_.
> ¹ Tuber; ² Yam
> **Derivatives:** _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#cikü|cikü]]_ ("red potato")
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kíkö|kíkö]]_
### kwilta
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kwiltɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kwɪɫdɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kwewdə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kwilta|*kwilta]]_, Perhaps related to [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kil|*kil]]_ ("tired, bored").
> ¹ Lazy
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#köda|köda]]_
### kyahyac'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kjɑˑçɑtʃʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kjɑɕɑtʃʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kjaɕətʃʼ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kyahyac'|*kyahyac']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kya-|*kya-]]_ ("suddenly or accidentally") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*hyac'|*hyac']]_ ("jump").
> ¹ To jump; ² To spring forward
### kyakop'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kjɑˑkopʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kjɑkɔpʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kjakɔpʼ]

> ¹ To burst
### kyak'ay
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kjɑˑqʼɑj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kjɑqʼɑj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kjaqʼaj]

> ¹ To fall off; ² To fall over; ³ To collapse
### kyak'öb
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kjɑˑkʼøb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kjɑkʼœb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kjakʼœb]

> ¹ To vomit
### kyalap'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kjɑˑlɑpʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kjɑlɑpʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kjaləpʼ]

### kyalwa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kjɑlwɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kjɑɫwɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kjawwə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kyalwa|*kyalwa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kyal|*kyal]]_ ("lay") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser").
> ¹ Laying flat on the ground
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kyova|kyova]]_
### kyanem
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kjɑˑnəm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kjɑnə̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kjanɛ̃ː]

### kyanit

> ¹ Idea
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kyanit|kyanit]]_
### kyanta
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kjɑntɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kjɑ̃ndɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kjɔ̃ndə]

> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kyonda|kyonda]]_
### kyat'ay
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kjɑˑtʼɑj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kjɑtʼɑj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kjatʼaj]

> ¹ To disappear
### kyawih
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kjɑˑwix]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kjɑwx]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kjawx]

### kyawik'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kjɑˑwikʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kjɑwkʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kjawkʼ]

> ¹ To change (suddenly or unexpectedly)
### kyawkyaw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kjɑwkjɑw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kjɑwkjɑw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kjawkjaw]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kyawkyaw|*kyawkyaw]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kyaw|*kyaw]]_ ("scream") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("repetitively").
> ¹ To caw, howl
# k'
### k'abah
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [qʼɑˑbɑχ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [qʼɑbɑχ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [qʼabəχ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*q'apah|*q'apah]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*q'a|*q'a]]_ ("peak").
> ¹ The mountains of [[T'ugü]]'
> **Derivatives:** _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#k'abahcüw|k'abahcüw]]_ ("öxp'a")
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kabah|kabah]]_
### k'abahcüw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [qʼɑˑbɑχtʃyw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [qʼɑbɑχtʃʏw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [qʼabəχtʃew]

*n.* From _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#k'abah|k'abah]]_ ("mountains") + _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#cüw|cüw]]_ ("cüo").
> ¹ A large wug, similar to terrestrial takin
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kabahco|kabahco]]_
### k'abk'ab
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [qʼɑbqʼɑb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [qʼɑbqʼɑb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [qʼabqʼəb]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'apk'ap|*k'apk'ap]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'ap|*k'ap]]_ ("sea mollusc") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("specifier").
> ¹ Any sea mollusc with an external shell
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kapkab|kapkab]]_

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'apk'ap|*k'apk'ap]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'ap|*k'ap]]_ ("sweat") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("directionless intransitive").
> ¹ To sweat
### k'ak'ohümi
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [qʼɑˑkʼoxʷymi]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [qʼɑkʼɔɸʏmɪ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [qʼakʼɔɸʏmɪ]

*n.* From [[High Alöbi]] _[[High Alöbi dictionary#q'aq'ugǖmi|q'aq'ugǖmi]]_, from _[[High Alöbi dictionary#q'aq'ug|q'aq'ug]]_ ("giant snail") + _[[High Alöbi dictionary#ǖm|ǖm]]_ ("wooden construction") + _[[High Alöbi dictionary#-i|-i]]_ ("relational linker"). Equivalent to _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#t'ak'og|t'ak'og]]_ ("giant snail") + _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#üm|üm]]_ ("wooden construction") + _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#-i|-i]]_ ("relational linker").
> ¹ A large wagon which can be inverted to form a temporary home, used in [[Öb#Seasonal migration|Öb seasonal migrations]]
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kakofmi|kakofmi]]_
### k'atbaü
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [qʼɑtbɑy]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [qʼɑdbɑj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [qʼadbaj]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'atpaǖ|*k'atpaǖ]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'at|*k'at]]_ ("base, bottom part") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*paǖ|*paǖ]]_ ("tree").
> ¹ Tree trunk, stump
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kadbe|kadbe]]_
### k'atem
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [qʼɑˑtəm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [qʼɑdə̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [qʼadɛ̃ː]

### k'ayam

### k'ayatem

> ¹ Base, bottom part
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#keden|keden]]_

> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kíya|kíya]]_
### k'ibik'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kʼiˑbikʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kʼibɪkʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kʼibɪkʼ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'ipik'|*k'ipik']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*q'ip|*q'ip]]_ ("rain").
> ¹ Raindrop

### k'icib
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kʼiˑtʃib]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kʼidʒɪb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kʼidʒɪb]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'icīp|*k'icīp]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'i-|*k'i-]]_ ("again") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*cīp|*cīp]]_ ("polish, sharpen").
> ¹ To polish; ² To sharpen, as of a blade
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kíji|kíji]]_
### k'ic'og
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kʼiˑtʃʼoŋ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kʼitʃʼɔ̃ŋ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kʼitʃʼɔ̃ː]

> ¹ Bamboo
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kícon|kícon]]_
### k'ilunön
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kʼiˑlunøn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kʼiɫnœ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kʼewnɔ̃ː]

> ¹ A spice made from the root of the [[K'unön]] plant
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#könon|könon]]_
### k'imaq

### k'imay

### k'iwa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kʼiˑwɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kʼiwɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kʼiwə]

### k'iwk'iw

### k'lablix

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'laplix|*k'laplix]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*q'lap'|*q'lap']]_ ("lightning, thunder") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*p'atlix|*p'atlix]]_ ("bright flash of light").

### k'unön

### k'übi

> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kíbi|kíbi]]_
### k'winta

### labet

### labina

### lablah
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑˑblɑχ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑblɑχ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [labləχ]

### liblib
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [liˑblib]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [liblɪb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [liblɪb]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*liplip|*liplip]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*lip|*lip]]_ ("trap") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("specifier").
> ¹ Fish trap
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#líblib|líblib]]_
### -lig

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-rig|*-rig]]_.
> ¹ Numeral classifier used to count long, thin objects such as sticks, rods and bones
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-lin|-lin]]_
### lihas

### maqmaq
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [mɑʔmɑʔ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [mɑʔmɑʔ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [maʔməʔ]

> ¹ To do the same thing over and over
### masaw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [mɑˑsɑw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [mɑsɑw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [masaw]

### maten

### myawa

### myawmö
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [mjɑwmø]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [mjɑwmœ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [mjawmœ]

*num.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*myawmü|*myawmü]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*umü|*umü]]_ ("five"). Perhaps related to [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*maq|*maq]]_ ("repeat").
> ¹ Twenty five (five squared)
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ñomö|ñomö]]_ ("twenty five")

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*myawmmü|*myawmmü]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*myawmü|*myawmü]]_ ("twenty five (five squared)") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*mü|*mü]]_ ("cycle").
> ¹ A calendar year, equal to 250 days
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ñomö|ñomö]]_
# n
### -na

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-na|*-na]]_.
> ¹ Numeral classifier used to count longish objects such as fish (dead, for eating), certain fruit, dead bodies, knives and planks of wood
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-na|-na]]_
### nacom
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [nɑˑtʃom]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [nɑdʒɔ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [nadʒɔ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*naʔcum|*naʔcum]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*naʔ|*naʔ]]_ ("time") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*cal|*cal]]_ ("boundary") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ A transitionary period
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#najon|najon]]_
### nalik
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [nɑˑlik]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [nɑɫk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [nawk]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*narīk|*narīk]]_.
> ¹ Penis
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#nok|nok]]_
### naliken
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [nɑˑlikən]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [nɑɫkə̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [nawkɛ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*narīken|*narīken]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*narīk|*narīk]]_ ("penis") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-en|*-en]]_ ("possessed").
> ¹ Male animal
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#noken|noken]]_
### nalikna
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [nɑˑliknɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [nɑɫknɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [nawknə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*narīkna|*narīkna]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*narīken|*narīken]]_ ("male animal").
> ¹ Male, of animals
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#nokna|nokna]]_
### nanekwa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [nɑˑnəkwɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [nɑnəkwɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [nanəkwə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*naʔneqwa|*naʔneqwa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*naʔ|*naʔ]]_ ("time") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*neq|*neq]]_ ("old") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser").
> ¹ Ancient
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#nankva|nankva]]_
### naniw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [nɑˑniw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [nɑnɪw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [nanew]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*nanyiw|*nanyiw]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<an>|*<an>]]_ ("instrument") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*nyiw|*nyiw]]_ ("twist, twine").
> ¹ Comb
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#nano|nano]]_
### naqem
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [nɑˑʔəm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [nɑʔə̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [naʔɛ̃ː]

### naqnaq
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [nɑʔnɑʔ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [nɑʔnɑʔ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [naʔnəʔ]

### nawnaw

### nayacay

### nayaem

### nayam

> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#nífmö|nífmö]]_ ("fourteen")
### nühö
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [nyˑxʷø]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [nyɸœ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [nyɸœ]

*num.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*nǖhü|*nǖhü]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*nǖh|*nǖh]]_ ("three").
> ¹ Three

> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#nífö|nífö]]_
### nühüsö
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [nyˑxʷysø]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [nyɸʏsœ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [nyɸʏsœ]

### nüta

### nyak'lap'

### oxam
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [oˑʃɑm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [oʃɑ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [oʃɔ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wuxam|*wuxam]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wu-|*wu-]]_ ("back and forth") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xam|*xam]]_ ("throw").
> ¹ To throw back and forth
### oxay
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [oˑʃɑj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [oʃɑj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [oʃaj]

# ö
### -ö

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*mü|*mü]]_ ("cycle"), from [[Proto-Upic language|Proto-Upic]] _[[Proto-Upic dictionary#\*mu|*mu]]_.
> ¹ Numeral classifier used to count cyclic objects such as wheels, months and years, as well as generations and things of a reciprocal nature such as transactions
### öb

> ¹ Tendon, sinew
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#pívo|pívo]]_
### p'lasa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [pʼlɑˑsɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [pʼlɑsɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [pʼlasə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*p'lasa|*p'lasa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*p'las|*p'las]]_ ("sparkle, shine, as of a star").
> ¹ Sparkling
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#plasa|plasa]]_
### p'lasabet
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [pʼlɑˑsɑbət]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [pʼlɑsɑbət]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [pʼlasəbət]

> ¹ Constellation
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#plaspat|plaspat]]_
### p'lasem

### p'löcem

### p'ülp'ül

# q

> ¹ To sift
### sota
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [soˑtɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [sodɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [sodə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*suta|*suta]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*sut|*sut]]_ ("blue, green"). Perhaps related to [[Xiri]] _[[Xiri dictionary#sō|sō]]_ ("blue").
> ¹ Blue, green
### sotcaic
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [sottʃɑitʃ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [sɔttʃɑjtʃ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [sɔttʃajtʃ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*sutcayic|*sutcayic]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*sut|*sut]]_ ("blue, green") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*cay|*cay]]_ ("pass by") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ic|*-ic]]_ ("agentive").
> ¹ A green comet which appears in Winter's sky every few centuries
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#sotcec|sotcec]]_

> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-sö|-sö]]_
### süca

### süm

> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#dönnat|dönnat]]_
### tömön
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tøˑmøn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tømœ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tømɔ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tümyün|*tümyün]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tü-|*tü-]]_ ("inchoative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*myün|*myün]]_ ("grow, increase").
> ¹ To sprout
### tönal
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tøˑnɑl]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tønɑɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tønaw]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tünal|*tünal]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tü-|*tü-]]_ ("inchoative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*nal|*nal]]_ ("awake").
> ¹ To wake up
### töniw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tøˑniw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tønɪw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tønew]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tünyiw|*tünyiw]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tü-|*tü-]]_ ("together") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*nyiw|*nyiw]]_ ("twist, twine").
> ¹ To twine; ² To twist
### tötob
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tøˑtob]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tødɔb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tødɔb]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tütup|*tütup]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tü-|*tü-]]_ ("together") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tup|*tup]]_ ("press").
> ¹ To press two things together
### tötyom
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tøˑcom]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tøɟɔ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tøɟɔ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tütyum|*tütyum]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tü-|*tü-]]_ ("together") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tyum|*tyum]]_ ("curl up").
> ¹ To curl up
### töwik'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tøˑwikʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tøwkʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tewkʼ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tüwik'|*tüwik']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tü-|*tü-]]_ ("inchoative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wik'|*wik']]_ ("different, change").
> ¹ To become
### töwin
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tøˑwin]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tøwɪ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tøwɪ̃ː]

### tük

### tüka

### tümnim

# t'
### t'aba
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʼɑˑbɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʼɑbɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʼabə]

> ¹ Smooth, slippery
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#taba|taba]]_
### t'ak'og
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʼɑˑkʼoŋ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʼɑkʼɔ̃ŋ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʼakʼɔ̃ː]

> ¹ [[K'ak'oh]], a giant snail endemic to [[T'ugü]]
> **Derivatives:** _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#k'ak'ohümi|k'ak'ohümi]]_ ("wagon house")
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#takon|takon]]_
### t'anik
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʼɑˑnik]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʼɑnɪk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʼanɪk]

### t'anök'

### t'ökt'ök'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʼøktʼøkʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʼœktʼœkʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʼœktʼœkʼ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ükt'ük'|*t'ükt'ük']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ük'|*t'ük']]_ ("chop up") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("repetitively").
> ¹ To chop up into pieces, as of meat
### t'uc'ah
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʼuˑtʃʼɑχ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʼutʃʼɑχ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʼutʃʼəχ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ūc'ah|*t'ūc'ah]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ū-|*t'ū-]]_ ("whole, entire") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*c'ah|*c'ah]]_ ("destroy").
> ¹ To destroy
### t'ugü
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʼuˑŋy]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʼuŋʏ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʼuŋʏ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ūgǖʔ|*t'ūgǖʔ]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ū-|*t'ū-]]_ ("whole, entire") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gǖʔ|*gǖʔ]]_ ("land").
> ¹ The [[T'ugü]] river basin, the entire world known to the [[Öb]] before contact with other cultures
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#túgö|túgö]]_
### t'umay
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʼuˑmɑj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʼumɑj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʼumaj]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ūmay|*t'ūmay]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ū-|*t'ū-]]_ ("whole, entire") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*may|*may]]_ ("know, remember").
> ¹ To understand; ² To realise
### t'ut'ik
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʼuˑtʼik]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʼutʼɪk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʼutʼɪk]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ūt'ik|*t'ūt'ik]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ū-|*t'ū-]]_ ("whole, entire") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ik|*t'ik]]_ ("cut").
> ¹ To cut off, decapitate
### t'ut'it
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʼuˑtʼit]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʼutʼɪt]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʼutʼɪt]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ūt'īt|*t'ūt'īt]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ū-|*t'ū-]]_ ("whole, entire") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ay|*t'ay]]_ ("be gone") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Total solar eclipse
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#tútit|tútit]]_
### t'ut'un
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʼuˑtʼun]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʼutʼʊ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʼutʼʊ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ūt'ūn|*t'ūt'ūn]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ū-|*t'ū-]]_ ("whole, entire") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ūn|*t'ūn]]_ ("amputate").
> ¹ To amputate
### t'uxiw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʼuˑʃiw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʼuʃɪw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʼuʃew]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ūxiw|*t'ūxiw]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ū-|*t'ū-]]_ ("whole, entire") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xiw|*xiw]]_ ("expel").
> ¹ To expel, drive away
# u
### -u

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ū|*-ū]]_.
> ¹ Numeral classifier used to count structureless or abstract objects such as thoughts, colours and sounds
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-u|-u]]_
### ua
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [uˑɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [uɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [uə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wūʔa|*wūʔa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wūʔ|*wūʔ]]_ ("good").
> ¹ Good, right; ² Fortunate
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#úva|úva]]_
### ubak
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [uˑbɑq]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ubɑq]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ubəq]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ūpak|*ūpak]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pak|*pak]]_ ("animal").
> ¹ Any wild land animal
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#úbak|úbak]]_
### ubay
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [uˑbɑj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ubɑj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ubaj]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ūppay|*ūppay]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ūp-|*ūp-]]_ ("surface") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pay|*pay]]_ ("layer").
> ¹ To layer on, as of paint

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ūpway|*ūpway]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ūp-|*ūp-]]_ ("surface") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*way|*way]]_ ("apply").
> ¹ To apply dye or varnish; ² To treat a wound
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#úbe|úbe]]_ ("to lacquer, apply")
### ubgü
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ubŋy]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʊbŋʏ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʊbŋʏ]

### ubkay

### ublüm
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [uˑblym]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ublʏ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ublʊ̃ː]

### uböt

### ubsöb
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ubsøb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʊbsœb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʊbsœb]

### ubt'ab
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ubtʼɑb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʊbtʼɑb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʊbtʼəb]

### ubxak'

### ubyan
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [uˑbjɑn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ubjɑ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ubjɔ̃ː]

> ¹ To cover over, as with a sheet
### ugo
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [uˑŋo]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [uŋɔ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [uŋɔ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ūgu|*ūgu]]_.
> ¹ [[Ugo]], a large domesticated ungulate used as a draft animal, similar to cattle
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#úgo|úgo]]_
### -uk

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ūk|*-ūk]]_.
> ¹ Numeral classifier used to count objects with a branching structure such as trees, pieces of [[Cimcim#Ökya cimcim|ökya cimcim]] and lightning bolts
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-uk|-uk]]_
### umab
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [uˑmɑb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [umɑb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [uməb]

> ¹ To roll out

ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [uˑmis]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [umɪs]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [umɪs]

### utok
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [uˑtok]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [udɔk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [udɔk]

# ü

### ükis

ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yˑlɑb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ylɑb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [yləb]

### ülan
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yˑlɑn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ylɑ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ylɔ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖran|*ǖran]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖ-|*ǖ-]]_ ("locative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ran|*ran]]_ ("on"). Perhaps related to [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖtyan|*ǖtyan]]_ ("near"), [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖyan|*ǖyan]]_ ("inside").
> ¹ To be on the surface of
### ülap'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yˑlɑpʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ylɑpʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [yləpʼ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖnlap'|*ǖnlap']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖn-|*ǖn-]]_ ("slowly and carefully") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*lap'|*lap']]_ ("grab, snatch").
> ¹ To take into the hand; ² To grab onto
### ülay
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yˑlɑj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ylɑj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ylaj]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖray|*ǖray]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖ-|*ǖ-]]_ ("locative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ray|*ray]]_ ("be in a place").
> ¹ To be at a place
### üm
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ym]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʏ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʊ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖm|*ǖm]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖ|*ǖ]]_ ("wood, wooden") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ A complex construction made from several pieces of wood
> **Derivatives:** _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#k'ak'ohümi|k'ak'ohümi]]_ ("wagon house")
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#un|un]]_
### ümöt'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yˑmøtʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ymœtʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ymœtʼ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖmwit'|*ǖmwit']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖ-|*ǖ-]]_ ("locative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*mwit'|*mwit']]_ ("different, other").
> ¹ To be or go somewhere else
### ümüm
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yˑmym]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ymʏ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ymʊ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yǖmyǖm|*yǖmyǖm]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yǖm|*yǖm]]_ ("container, pot") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("specifier").
> ¹ Container, pot
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ímun|ímun]]_
### üncaw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yntʃɑw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʏ̃ndʒɑw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʊ̃ndʒaw]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖncaw|*ǖncaw]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖn-|*ǖn-]]_ ("slowly and carefully") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*caw|*caw]]_ ("deform").
> ¹ To physically deform
### ünih
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yˑnix]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ynɪx]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ynɪx]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖnih|*ǖnih]]_, Perhaps related to [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*rih|*rih]]_ ("point").
> ¹ Finger
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ínih|ínih]]_
### ünkay
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ynqɑj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʏ̃ɴqɑj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʊ̃ɴqaj]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖnkay|*ǖnkay]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖn-|*ǖn-]]_ ("slowly and carefully") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kay|*kay]]_ ("support").
> ¹ To balance on
### ünöm
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yˑnøm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ynœ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ynɔ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖnyüm|*ǖnyüm]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖn-|*ǖn-]]_ ("slowly and carefully") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yüm|*yüm]]_ ("hold, secure").
> ¹ To hold firmly in the hands
### üntil
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yntil]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʏ̃ndɪɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʊ̃ndew]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖntil|*ǖntil]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖn-|*ǖn-]]_ ("slowly and carefully") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*til|*til]]_ ("approach").
> ¹ To approach carefully, as when hunting an animal
### ünü
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yˑny]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ynʏ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ynʏ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖnʔǖ|*ǖnʔǖ]]_.
> ¹ Any fish
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ínö|ínö]]_
### üqüt
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yˑʔyt]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [yʔʏt]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [yʔʏt]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖʔǖt|*ǖʔǖt]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖ-|*ǖ-]]_ ("locative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔǖt|*ʔǖt]]_ ("back, behind").
> ¹ To be behind
### üsö
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yˑsø]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ysœ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ysœ]

*num.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔǖsü|*ʔǖsü]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔǖs|*ʔǖs]]_ ("ten").
> ¹ Ten
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ísö|ísö]]_
### üt
ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʏt]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʏt]

*n.* From _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#üta|üta]]_ ("bent, curved").
> ¹ Bow
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#öt|öt]]_
### üta
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yˑtɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ydɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ydə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yǖta|*yǖta]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yaw|*yaw]]_ ("enclose") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Enclosed
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ída|ída]]_

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yǖta|*yǖta]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yaw|*yaw]]_ ("bend") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Bent, curved
> **Derivatives:** _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#üt|üt]]_ ("bow")
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ída|ída]]_
### ütöl
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yˑtøl]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ydœɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ydew]

> ¹ To be in front of
### ütyan
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yˑcɑn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [yɟɑ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [yɟɔ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖtyan|*ǖtyan]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖ-|*ǖ-]]_ ("locative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tyan|*tyan]]_ ("near"). Perhaps related to [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖran|*ǖran]]_ ("on"), [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖyan|*ǖyan]]_ ("inside").
> ¹ To be within reach; ² To be directly next to
### üwac
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yˑwɑtʃ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ywɑtʃ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ywətʃ]

> ¹ To be far away from
### üxk'ab
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yʃqʼɑb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʏʃqʼɑb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʏʃqʼəb]

> ¹ Sea mollusc shell

### üxöm
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yˑʃøm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [yʃœ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [yʃɔ̃ː]

> ¹ To be downhill, downstream of; ² To be after
### üxt'ak'

### üyal
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yˑjɑl]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [yjɑɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [yjaw]

> ¹ To be in the middle of
### üyan
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yˑjɑn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [yjɑ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [yjɔ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖyan|*ǖyan]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖ-|*ǖ-]]_ ("locative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yan|*yan]]_ ("within, inside"). > ¹ To be inside of

### wack'ic

### wibiwmü
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [wiˑbiwmy]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [wibɪwmʏ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [wibewmʏ]

> ¹ To change (as a person)
### wik'ob
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [wiˑkʼob]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [wikʼɔb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [wikʼɔb]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wik'up|*wik'up]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wik'|*wik']]_ ("different, change") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ep|*-ep]]_ ("person object nominaliser").
> ¹ Foreigner
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#víkob|víkob]]_

### xöma
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃøˑmɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃømɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃømə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xümwa|*xümwa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xüm|*xüm]]_ ("downstream of, before") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser").
> ¹ Downstream; ² Later
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#xöma|xöma]]_

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xümwa|*xümwa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xüm|*xüm]]_ ("hide") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser").
> ¹ Hidden; ² Unknown
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#xöma|xöma]]_
### xömom
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃøˑmom]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃømɔ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃømɔ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xümum|*xümum]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xüm|*xüm]]_ ("downstream of, before") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Later point; ² Successor
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#xömon|xömon]]_

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xümum|*xümum]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xüm|*xüm]]_ ("hide") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Something unknown
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#xömon|xömon]]_
### xömxöm
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃømʃøm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃœ̃nʃœ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃɔ̃ːʃɔ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xümxüm|*xümxüm]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xüm|*xüm]]_ ("hide") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("directionless intransitive").
> ¹ To hide; ² To store
### xubxub
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃubʃub]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃʊbʃʊb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃʊbʃʊb]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xūpxūp|*xūpxūp]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xūp|*xūp]]_ ("adze") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("repetitively").
> ¹ To scrape out material, as with an adze
### xulab
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃuˑlɑb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃulɑb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃuləb]

> ¹ To tie into a bundle; ² To wrap around tightly

### xuniw

### xutyom

### yabek
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [jɑˑbək]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jɑbək]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jabək]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yapek|*yapek]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yap|*yap]]_ ("squeeze") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ek|*-ek]]_ ("animate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Insect larva
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#yabak|yabak]]_, [[Xiri]] _[[Xiri dictionary#yaba|yaba]]_

### yacwa

> ¹ To soak
### yok'i
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [joˑkʼi]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jokʼɪ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jokʼɪ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yuk'i|*yuk'i]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yu-|*yu-]]_ ("passively") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'i|*k'i]]_ ("hang, swing").
> ¹ To be hanging
### yola
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [joˑlɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jolɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jolə]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yura|*yura]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ur>|*<ur>]]_ ("quick and repetitive for a short time") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ya|*ya]]_ ("displace").
> ¹ To shake
### yolac
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [joˑlɑtʃ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jolɑtʃ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jolətʃ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yurac|*yurac]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ur>|*<ur>]]_ ("quick and repetitive for a short time") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yac|*yac]]_ ("joy").
> ¹ To laugh
### yolwa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [jolwɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jɔɫwɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jowwə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yurwa|*yurwa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ur>|*<ur>]]_ ("quick and repetitive for a short time") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ya|*ya]]_ ("displace") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser").
> ¹ Shaking, shivering
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#yúva|yúva]]_
### yomih
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [joˑmix]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jomɪx]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jomɪx]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yumih|*yumih]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yu-|*yu-]]_ ("passively") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*mih|*mih]]_ ("live").
> ¹ To live; ² To be free
### yomök
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [joˑmøk]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jomœk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jomœk]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yumük|*yumük]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yu-|*yu-]]_ ("passively") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*mük|*mük]]_ ("experience, witness").
> ¹ To experience
### yosol
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [joˑsol]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [josɔɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [josow]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yusur|*yusur]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yu-|*yu-]]_ ("passively") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*sur|*sur]]_ ("submerge").
> ¹ To sink
### yotas
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [joˑtɑs]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jodɑs]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jodəs]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yutas|*yutas]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yu-|*yu-]]_ ("passively") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tas|*tas]]_ ("dry").
> ¹ To dry out
### yoxok
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [joˑʃok]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [joʃɔk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [joʃɔk]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yuxuk|*yuxuk]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yu-|*yu-]]_ ("passively") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xuk|*xuk]]_ ("crumble").
> ¹ To decay; ² To crumble away
### yoxöm
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [joˑʃøm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [joʃœ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [joʃɔ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yuxüm|*yuxüm]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yu-|*yu-]]_ ("passively") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xüm|*xüm]]_ ("hide").
> ¹ To become obscured
### yua
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [juˑɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [juɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [juə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yūʔa|*yūʔa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yūʔ|*yūʔ]]_ ("scale").
> ¹ Scaly
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#yúva|yúva]]_
### yuek
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [juˑək]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [juk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [juk]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yūʔek|*yūʔek]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yūʔ|*yūʔ]]_ ("scale") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ek|*-ek]]_ ("animate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Any scaly fish
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#yuk|yuk]]_
### yunam
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [juˑnɑm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [junɑ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [junɔ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yūnam|*yūnam]]_.
> ¹ [[Yunam]], a large ungulate, similar to antelopes
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#yúnon|yúnon]]_
### yup'üh
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [juˑpʼyxʷ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jupʼʏɸ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jupʼʏɸ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yūp'ǖh|*yūp'ǖh]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*p'ǖh|*p'ǖh]]_ ("swarm").
> ¹ To swarm; ² To envelope
### yuso
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [juˑso]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jusɔ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jusɔ]

*pron.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yūsu|*yūsu]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*i-|*i-]]_ ("singular") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*usu|*usu]]_ ("second person").
> ¹ Second person singular
### yuyu
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [juˑju]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jujʊ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jujʊ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yūʔyūʔ|*yūʔyūʔ]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yūʔ|*yūʔ]]_ ("scale") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("specifier").
> ¹ Scales, as of fish or a lizard
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#yúyu|yúyu]]_
